<p><a href = vnd.unilang:adapted.html>Adapted</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">aquaeductus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">conveyance <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:water.html>water</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:aqua.html>aqua</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:water.html>water</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dūcō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> lead”, “I <a href = vnd.unilang:bring.html>bring</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">aqueduc</i>.

annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arkhi-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = lang="grc">πέλαγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pélagos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sea.html>sea</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> Aegean (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Arcipelago</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = = vnd.unilang:extension.html>extension</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> Arcipelago</i> <a href = <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:arend.html>arend</a> (14667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aernt</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:aren.html>aren</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*aro</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arô</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:help.html>help</a> Wiktionary <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> elaborating <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> origins <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a>.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arend.html>arend</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arenden.html>arenden</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arend.html>arendje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
